362→\t}\n   363→\n   364→\tfor tset, targets := range mc.TargetsGatherer.TargetsActive() {\n   365→\t\tvar size, length int\n   366→\t\tfor _, t := range targets {\n   367→\t\t\tsize += 373→\t\t\tprometheus.GaugeValue,\n   374→\t\t\tfloat64(length),\n   375→\t\t\ttset,\n   376→\t\t)\n   377→\n   378→\t\tch <- prometheus.MustNewConstMetric(\n   379→\t\t\tmc.CacheBytes,\n   380→\t\t\tprometheus.GaugeValue,\n   381→\t\t\tfloat64(size),\n   382→\t\t\ttset,\n   383→\t\t)\n   384→\t}\n   385→}\n   386→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider
